## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Envoy gRPC Health Check Protocol Compliance

## Your Task

Find all C++ source files in envoyproxy/envoy that implement gRPC health check protocol compliance: the grpc.health.v1.Health service implementation, the HealthCheckRequest handling, and the health check response status mapping.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the compliance domain.

## Available Resources

## gRPC Health Check Protocol Compliance in Envoy

### Primary Implementation Files

**`source/extensions/health_checkers/grpc/health_checker_impl.h`** — Declares:
- `GrpcHealthCheckerFactory` — registered factory for `envoy.health_checkers.grpc`
- `GrpcHealthCheckerImpl` — main checker class with `grpc.health.v1.Health.Check` method descriptor
- `GrpcActiveHealthCheckSession` — per-host session implementing `Http::ResponseDecoder`
- `ProdGrpcHealthCheckerImpl` — production subclass creating real HTTP/2 codec clients

**`source/extensions/health_checkers/grpc/health_checker_impl.cc`** — Implements:
1. **grpc.health.v1.Health service**: Constructor looks up `grpc.health.v1.Health.Check` from Protobuf descriptor pool
2. **HealthCheckRequest handling** (`onInterval()`): Creates `grpc::health::v1::HealthCheckRequest`, sets optional `service` field, serializes as gRPC frame over HTTP/2
3. **Response decoding** (`decodeHeaders()`, `decodeData()`, `decodeTrailers()`): Validates gRPC response, parses `grpc::health::v1::HealthCheckResponse`
4. **Status mapping** (`isHealthCheckSucceeded()`, `logHealthCheckStatus()`): Maps SERVING→healthy, NOT_SERVING/UNKNOWN/SERVICE_UNKNOWN→unhealthy

### Supporting Infrastructure Files
- `source/common/upstream/health_checker_impl.cc/.h` — `HealthCheckerFactory::create()` dispatches gRPC health check config
- `source/extensions/health_checkers/common/health_checker_base_impl.cc/.h` — `HealthCheckerImplBase` base class with timer-driven health check loop
